<!DOCTYPE HTML PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD HTML 4.0 Transitional//EN"><html lang="en-US"><head><title>EdgarFiling</title><meta content="text/html; charset=windows-1252" ><meta name="GENERATOR" content="MSHTML 8.00.7601.18094" ></head><body bgcolor="#ffffff"><p style="text-align: right;"><strong>EXHIBIT 99.1</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><strong>MiNK Therapeutics Reports Third Quarter 2024 Results and Business Update</strong></font></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong></strong></p><p>
             <p align="left">NEW YORK, Nov.  14, 2024  (GLOBE NEWSWIRE) -- MiNK Therapeutics, Inc.&#160;(NASDAQ: INKT), a clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company pioneering the discovery, development, and commercialization of allogeneic, off-the-shelf, invariant natural killer T (iNKT) cell therapies to treat cancer and other immune-mediated diseases, today announced results for the third quarter 2024. MiNK will host a conference call and webcast at&#160;8:30 a.m. ET.</p>              <p>&#8220;Our progress this quarter reflects MiNK&#8217;s commitment to advancing effective and scalable therapies in cancer and immune-mediated diseases,&#8221; said Jennifer Buell, PhD, Chief Executive Officer of MiNK Therapeutics. &#8220;We have continued to expand our iNKT cell therapy platform and partnerships to address high-need areas, recently showcasing the versatility of iNKT cells in two presentations at SITC. Our clinical programs are advancing with the ongoing Phase 2 study in second-line and later-stage gastric cancer, with initial data anticipated early next year. These developments underscore our momentum in delivering impactful treatments for patients.&#8221;</p>              <p><strong>Recent Business Updates: </strong></p>              <ul type="disc"><li style="margin-bottom:8pt;"><strong>Board Appointment:</strong> Dr. Robert Kadlec, a recognized authority in biodefense, pandemic preparedness, and public health strategy, has joined MiNK&#8217;s Board of Directors. Dr. Kadlec&#8217;s expertise in public health and biodefense will support MiNK&#8217;s iNKT cell platform in addressing critical infectious diseases.</li><li style="margin-bottom:8pt;"><strong>Research Collaboration:</strong> MiNK and Autonomous Therapeutics, a pioneer in disease-activated RNA medicines, entered into a research collaboration to target and treat metastatic tumors. The collaboration combines Autonomous&#8217; encrypted RNA&#153; (encRNA) technology with MiNK&#8217;s iNKT cell therapies, MiNK-215 and agenT-797, with the goal of developing therapies to effectively target metastatic cancer cells.</li><li style="margin-bottom:8pt;"><strong>SITC 2024 Presentations:</strong> Two poster presentations at the Society for Cancer Immunotherapy (SITC) 2024 Annual Meeting highlighted the potential of iNKT cell therapies in advancing cancer treatment:        <ul type="circle"><li style="margin-bottom:8pt;">AgenT-797 demonstrated enhanced activity of checkpoint inhibitors and bispecific engagers in combination.</li><li style="margin-bottom:8pt;">PRAME-targeted TCR iNKT cell therapy showcased the potential to address limitations of traditional T cell therapies in targeting solid tumors such as NSCLC, ovarian cancer, melanoma, and sarcoma. Preclinical studies indicate that PRAME-TCR-iNKTs can specifically target and kill tumor cells.</li></ul>        </li><li style="margin-bottom:8pt;"><strong>Solid Tumor Clinical Program:</strong> AgenT-797 is advancing in an enrolling Phase 2 trial in second-line and later-stage advanced gastroesophageal cancer at Memorial Sloan-Kettering Cancer Center, with results expected at a major conference in early 2025.</li><li style="margin-bottom:8pt;"><strong>Graft-versus-Host Disease (GvHD) Program: </strong>MiNK is advancing initiation of Phase 1 trial with external financial support to investigate agenT-797 for the treatment of GvHD, in collaboration with leading research institutions in the U.S. and EU for dosing to start in 2025.<br ></li></ul>              <p><strong>Financial Results</strong></p>              <p>MiNK ended the quarter with a cash balance of $6.3 million reflecting cash used in operations for the three and nine months ended September 2024 of $3 million and $7.8 million, respectively, reduced from $7.8 million and $12.7 million, for the same period in 2023.</p>              <p>Net loss for the three and nine months ended September 30, 2024, was $1.8 million, or $0.05 per share, and $8.3 million, or $0.22 per share, respectively. This compares to $5.1 million, or $0.15 per share, and $17 million or $0.50 per share, for the same periods in 2023.</p>       <table style="width:100%; border-collapse:collapse !important;;border-collapse: collapse; "><tr><td colspan="16" style="text-align: center ;  vertical-align: middle; vertical-align: bottom ; "><strong>Summary Consolidated Financial Information</strong></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8" style="vertical-align: bottom ;
